  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_47fa702a-950a-4605-a59f-2424564b7449'

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2117411161?book_show_action=true">Jul 05, 2019</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Meredith" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Meredith" href="/user/show/30978160-meredith">Meredith</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/12871681-third-grave-dead-ahead">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/30978160-meredith?shelf=overdrive">overdrive</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2117411161" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8913693646132973636"><i>
  <b>“There comes a moment when you know you just aren’t going to do anything else productive for the rest of the day.” </b>
</i><br/><br/>I needed a quick pick-me-up, so I thought why not turn to my favorite grim reaper, Charley Davidson! <br/><br/>Book 3 picks up shortly after the events of book 2. Charley must deal with the fallout from what she did to Reyes. She also must stay awake to avoid intimate encounters with the son of Satan, so she has been awake for almost two weeks, which does not put her in the best state of </span>
  <span id="freeText8913693646132973636" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>“There comes a moment when you know you just aren’t going to do anything else productive for the rest of the day.” </b>
</i><br /><br />I needed a quick pick-me-up, so I thought why not turn to my favorite grim reaper, Charley Davidson! <br /><br />Book 3 picks up shortly after the events of book 2. Charley must deal with the fallout from what she did to Reyes. She also must stay awake to avoid intimate encounters with the son of Satan, so she has been awake for almost two weeks, which does not put her in the best state of mind. At the same time, she picks up the case of a missing woman. Needless to say, things get out of hand rather quickly! <br /><br />As always, this series brings witty and quirky characters. It’s fast, fun and easy to read. The ending leaves Charley with some intriguing decisions to make. I loved the addition of Artemis, and I can’t wait to see what’s next for Charley, Cookie, and all of the other crazies who make this series so much fun to read! <br /><br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="8913693646132973636" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5210022-julie?shelf=netgalley">netgalley</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5210022-julie?shelf=e-book">e-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5210022-julie?shelf=2018">2018</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2591153524" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2428538066265395659">Third Grave Dead Ahead by Darynda Jones is a 2012 St. Martin’s Press publication. <br/><br/>This third installment in the Charley Davidson series deals with the fallout from the controversial conclusion of book two. <br/><br/>Let’s just say Reyes a quivering with rage and leave it at that. Meanwhile, Charley’s father tries to convince Charley to find a new occupation, while she tackles a missing persons case. Not only that, Charley faces the irony of dealing with a motorcycle gang, along with Reyes’ unrelenting adv</span>
  <span id="freeText2428538066265395659" style="display:none">Third Grave Dead Ahead by Darynda Jones is a 2012 St. Martin’s Press publication. <br /><br />This third installment in the Charley Davidson series deals with the fallout from the controversial conclusion of book two. <br /><br />Let’s just say Reyes a quivering with rage and leave it at that. Meanwhile, Charley’s father tries to convince Charley to find a new occupation, while she tackles a missing persons case. Not only that, Charley faces the irony of dealing with a motorcycle gang, along with Reyes’ unrelenting advances- which leaves her living on caffeine and adrenaline. <br /><br />This installment settles down just a little, although it is still very chaotic. While still humorous and action packed, but the high pitched emotional edge didn’t carry over from book two. This one felt more like a standard procedural, although there were still a few very interesting developments with Reyes which includes a worrisome revelation. Reyes, is a bit too aggressive for my taste, although he has pushed the envelope of consent from the get- go. For some reason, that really stood out in this third book, and made me squirm a little. <br /><br />Other than that, this is still a solid addition to the series, and I’m still on board for book four. <br />3.5 stars<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="2428538066265395659" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/160757252" />
    <a title="Suzanne (Doppleganger)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1365925-suzanne-doppleganger"><img alt="Suzanne (Doppleganger)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1259351688p2/1365925.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/160757252?book_show_action=true">Apr 13, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Suzanne (Doppleganger)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Suzanne (Doppleganger)" href="/user/show/1365925-suzanne-doppleganger">Suzanne (Doppleganger)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/12871681-third-grave-dead-ahead">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1365925-suzanne-doppleganger?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1365925-suzanne-doppleganger?shelf=ghosts">ghosts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1365925-suzanne-doppleganger?shelf=funny">funny</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer160757252" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10476341479609488549">This book was fabulous! I can honestly say I loved every single page, and not because of Charley's severe coffee addiction. That's just a bonus. <br/><br/>I loved this book because Charley gets funnier, Reyes shows more of his hot devilish side, Cookie and Charley have the most hysterical dialogue, and Wong is...still in the corner. <br/><br/>Somewhere about halfway into Third Grave it hit me that I was completely wrapped up in the plot. Charley isn't just the grim reaper, Reyes' love interest, or a crazy woman in </span>
  <span id="freeText10476341479609488549" style="display:none">This book was fabulous! I can honestly say I loved every single page, and not because of Charley's severe coffee addiction. That's just a bonus. <br /><br />I loved this book because Charley gets funnier, Reyes shows more of his hot devilish side, Cookie and Charley have the most hysterical dialogue, and Wong is...still in the corner. <br /><br />Somewhere about halfway into Third Grave it hit me that I was completely wrapped up in the plot. Charley isn't just the grim reaper, Reyes' love interest, or a crazy woman in search of her next coffee fix. She's a P.I. with some serious chops for the job. I didn't realize I was paying attention! I was laughing so much that it took me by surprise to find an honest-to-goodness mystery in the middle of all that comedy. <br /><br />Then at ~85% through the book, about when I'd adjusted to the concept of a mystery in my comedy, this emotional depth crept in and I got whalloped with it's intensity. Hiding the emotional content behind the comedy was sneaky as hell, but also extremely effective. It made the emotional whallop hit harder. <br /><br />My reactions to this book can be summed up like this:<br />Smile, laugh, giggle, awwww, gasp, guffaw, P*SSED!, snort, swoon, WTF?, laugh, cry cry cry, WOW.<br /><br />Yes, you read that correctly. I 'guffawed'. Out loud. <br /><br />Well played, Ms. Jones. 5 stars. <br /><br />I'd give an extra-credit star for the coffee if I could.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="10476341479609488549" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

She is also suspicious that this guy will try and kill her too when he realizes that she knows the truth. Of course he's going to try and kill you! Everyone tries to kill Charley. <div id="review_3008053791" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">

    <a title="Phrynne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8655084-phrynne"><img alt="Phrynne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1577753809p2/8655084.jpg" /></a>

<div id="review_220136304" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/220136304" />
    <a title="Giselle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4800103-giselle"><img alt="Giselle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1310159877p2/4800103.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/220136304?book_show_action=true">Oct 07, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Giselle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Giselle" href="/user/show/4800103-giselle">Giselle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4800103-giselle?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4800103-giselle?shelf=own">own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer220136304" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3859121919693626510"><b>
  <i>"Death comes to those who wait. And to those who don't. So either way…"</i>
</b><br/><br/>I could never get tired of our dear Charley Davidson. First Grave on the Right and Second Grave on the Left were both incredibly funny and smart. Third Grave Dead Ahead is no exception. It only took about 10 pages for me to be falling off my chair laughing.<br/><br/>The plot in Third Grave Dead Ahead is similar to the others. Charley gets a case; trying to find a missing person, while dealing with Reyes and the other pain in the bu</span>
  <span id="freeText3859121919693626510" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>"Death comes to those who wait. And to those who don't. So either way…"</i>
</b><br /><br />I could never get tired of our dear Charley Davidson. First Grave on the Right and Second Grave on the Left were both incredibly funny and smart. Third Grave Dead Ahead is no exception. It only took about 10 pages for me to be falling off my chair laughing.<br /><br />The plot in Third Grave Dead Ahead is similar to the others. Charley gets a case; trying to find a missing person, while dealing with Reyes and the other pain in the butt men in her life. The mystery behind the case isn't particularly hard to decipher. I had most of it figured out well before the end. But this book isn't to be read for the suspense behind the plot; read this for the incredible characters and especially entertaining dialogue. Don't get me wrong, the case is still fun, but the characters make the show.<br /><br />I can't say enough about the personalities in this series. Charley is, as always, witty, sarcastic and incredibly hilarious. I love how she takes everything lightly in grave situations. It doesn't only get her into trouble, it also makes her brave - which is a must for a PI. And don't fret, Danger and Will also make a few appearances. Her best friend and receptionist, Cookie, is equally entertaining, and she complements Charley like a hand and glove. We meet a few new characters as well that make a great addition to the story. I'm not sure what's going to occur with Donovan, but I'm positive it'll be pretty amusing. At least before it all goes to hell - yes the hell. As for Charley's dad, I don't really understand the length he went through to try to get his way in this novel. I'm getting a bit annoyed by him - he's not very nice, especially after painting a target on Charley's back in the previous book.<br /><br />Now... Reyes *sigh*, he's more present than in Second Grave on the Left, but he still hasn't really joined the cast of main characters. The coming apocalypse storyline also doesn't progress much. I'm hoping when it does we'll get to see more of him. On the other hand, we did get answers to a few burning questions I had from the previous books: Mistress Marigold and Owen Vaughn. I didn't expect to get both of those revelations in this one , so I was very pleased. I think Owen is a bit psychotic: I understand what happened was awful but to the point of attempted murder…? So I doubt we've seen the last of him.<br /><br />Third Grave Dead Ahead is no insignificant installment. It's fun, funny and full of charm. If you've enjoyed Charley before, you'll definitely enjoy her again in this one!<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"How would you feel about us becoming plumbers? I have a nice crack."</i>
</b><br /><br />--<br />For more of my reviews, visit my blog at <a href="http://www.xpressoreads.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Xpresso Reads</b>
</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="3859121919693626510" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_199858927" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/199858927" />
    <a title="Dija" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2857113-dija"><img alt="Dija" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1360335537p2/2857113.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/199858927?book_show_action=true">Aug 18, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dija" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dija" href="/user/show/2857113-dija">Dija</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Dija by: </span>
      The cover
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=read-in-2012">read-in-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=jan-2012">jan-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=childhood-friends-turned-lovers">childhood-friends-turned-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=uf-or-pnr">uf-or-pnr</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=my-harem">my-harem</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=my-reviews">my-reviews</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2857113-dija?shelf=lollercoaster">lollercoaster</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer199858927" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2542060157025258936">The UF genre needs more series like Charley Davidson, and more heroines like Charley. Series like this are the reason I became obsessed with the genre in the first place. Series that make me seriously entertain the thought of an alternate world out there, one where <s>the Son of Satan</s> grim reapers, werewolves, vampires, angels, and the whole lot run free. I've always considered a healthy belief in "What if's" to be essential for one's mental growth, so no, I'm not at all concerned about my sanity a</span>
  <span id="freeText2542060157025258936" style="display:none">The UF genre needs more series like Charley Davidson, and more heroines like Charley. Series like this are the reason I became obsessed with the genre in the first place. Series that make me seriously entertain the thought of an alternate world out there, one where <s>the Son of Satan</s> grim reapers, werewolves, vampires, angels, and the whole lot run free. I've always considered a healthy belief in "What if's" to be essential for one's mental growth, so no, I'm not at all concerned about my sanity after writing that. <br /><br /><i>Third Grave Dead Ahead</i> focuses more on the relationship between Charley and Reyes than the previous books. There's more on Charley's background and her "powers" here as well. Another love interest is also introduced, converting the love triangle to a harem instead (not that I'm complaining, mind you. Charley deserves all the love.) <br /><br />Speaking of, Charley is my role model. I aspire to be as lively, witty, strong, and brilliant as her. I have half a mind to simply quote all the passages I loved, present them as evidence for why Charley is the funniest UF heroine in creation, and leave it at that. But since I never miss the chance to gush about her, I'll add a "few" words. This book took a dramatic turn towards the end, and I'm amazed at how well Charley dealt with it. She convincingly proved that not only is she humorous, she can also be clever and mature when the situation calls for it. It's remarkable how she can manage to be so funny without seeming like an airhead in the least. <br /><br />So after all that praise, why is this still a 4-star book? Only because of one simply rule I have when it comes to giving 5 stars: if I have to take out the time to <i>think</i> about whether or not I loved a book enough to give it that rating, I won't. Because that thinking part alone means there was something missing, some sort of epic factor found in the other books I've rated 5 stars, that wasn't present here. Maybe I can't pinpoint it at the moment, but it usually comes to me the next time I give that high rating.<br /><br />Nonetheless, I LOVE this series. I feel the need to strongly emphasize this point again, especially after the previous paragraph. Charley Davidson (the series, not the character) is refreshing, exciting, original, and thoroughly engaging. It takes immense talent to turn everything into a joke at one moment and to reveal something serious or tragic the next. This is a light and funny book for the most part, but it has these great heart-wrenching, thought-provoking moments that do more for the series than all the jokes combined. And I think <i>that</i>, more than anything else, is what makes Dyranda Jones's writing style stand out against all the other UF authors out there. <br /><br /><b>My love letter to Reyes (SPOILERS AHEAD!):</b><br /><br />Because of the way Third Grave ended, I composed a <i>very</i> friendly letter to Reyes and mailed it to his address within the depths of Hell. Here's a copy:<br /><blockquote>Smexy Reyes,<br /><br />You <i>know</i> how much I love you, how I positively swoon every time you appear, and how I would even give up chocolate if it meant we could be together. But sweetie, you have <i>got</i> to stop playing these mind games with Charley, putting her in danger, keeping secrets from her, and hitting her. I'm sure you have your reasons, but until you put an end to this infuriating habit of yours...let me just remind you that she will always come first for me, even if you're hotter, and the next time you mess with her, I'll lock her up with Donovan and/or Garrett in a secluded bedroom and let lust run its natural course. How would you like <i>that</i>? My thoughts precisely. Now get your act together, and grovel at <s>my</s> Charley's feet, or I <i>will</i> execute this brilliant plan of mine. <br /><br />Courageously, <br />Dija</blockquote><br /><b>Some of my favorite quotes:</b><br /><blockquote>Puppy love was a powerful elixir. I should know. The things I did for Tim La Croix, my senior-year crush. Unfortunately, I’d been in kindergarten at the time, otherwise he might have taken note.<br /><br />When everything is coming your way, you’re in the wrong lane.<br />—T-SHIRT<br /><br />Reyes hit me! He’d actually hit me! It didn’t matter that hitting me wasn’t really like hitting a regular girl and I’d be completely healed in a matter of hours. I was still a freaking girl, and he damned well knew it. I’d just have to hit him back. With a lead pipe. Or an eighteen-wheeler.<br /><br /><i>“The top five things you never want to say to a grim reaper: I’m dead tired. You’re killing me. I’m dying to try that. This relationship will be the death of me.<br />[...]<br />The number one thing you don’t want to say to the grim reaper is…Till death do us part.”</i></blockquote><br /><b>4.5/5 stars</b><br /><br /><b>For more reviews, visit my <a href="http://zombiehazard.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">blog</a>. </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2542060157025258936" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

    <a title="Carolyn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19559507-carolyn"><img alt="Carolyn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1546411572p2/19559507.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/3025560403?book_show_action=true">Jun 14, 2020</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carolyn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carolyn" href="/user/show/19559507-carolyn">Carolyn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17309968-third-grave-dead-ahead">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19559507-carolyn?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19559507-carolyn?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19559507-carolyn?shelf=2020">2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19559507-carolyn?shelf=private-investigator">private-investigator</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3025560403" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7498664668396868908">I'm starting to feel a bit conflicted with this series. I like sassy, smart-mouthed Charley and really like her role as the Grim Reaper, an entity that can be used by departed souls to cross to the other side, which means she meets some very interesting souls. It also makes her job as a PI interesting when she can use ghosts to tail suspects or find out if someone is dead. However, I found her constant wisecracking a bit heavy handed, particularly early in the book and for a smart girl she does </span>
  <span id="freeText7498664668396868908" style="display:none">I'm starting to feel a bit conflicted with this series. I like sassy, smart-mouthed Charley and really like her role as the Grim Reaper, an entity that can be used by departed souls to cross to the other side, which means she meets some very interesting souls. It also makes her job as a PI interesting when she can use ghosts to tail suspects or find out if someone is dead. However, I found her constant wisecracking a bit heavy handed, particularly early in the book and for a smart girl she does make some stupid decisions. I'm also not that into her relationship with Reyes, the son of Satan, which seems to be entirely based on lust, even though he is currently very angry with Charley. As well as taking on an interesting missing person's case, Charley also goes looking for witnesses to the murder case that landed Reyes in jail and soon lands herself in a heap of trouble. I'm thinking I'll give the series one more chance and see if book 4 gives some idea where this is all heading. 3.5★</span>
  <a data-text-id="7498664668396868908" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_431525929" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/431525929" />
    <a title="VampireNovelFan" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4897902-vampirenovelfan"><img alt="VampireNovelFan" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1296445543p2/4897902.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/431525929?book_show_action=true">Oct 10, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="VampireNovelFan" class="user" itemprop="url" name="VampireNovelFan" href="/user/show/4897902-vampirenovelfan">VampireNovelFan</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780749956141" href="/book/show/10980787-third-grave-dead-ahead">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4897902-vampirenovelfan?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4897902-vampirenovelfan?shelf=urban-fantasy">urban-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4897902-vampirenovelfan?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4897902-vampirenovelfan?shelf=wish-i-dnf">wish-i-dnf</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer431525929" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13127972336371327309"><a href='http://vampirenovelfan.wordpress.com/2012/10/14/third-grave-dead-ahead-charley-davidson-3-dead-on-arrival/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <b>Dead on Arrival…</b>
</a><br/><br/>I’m starting to wonder how many more directions we’ll get to these graves. Right, left, ahead… I don’t even know if Charley knows where she’s going anymore. I just hope the cemetery isn’t that big. Personally, I just want to know the directions to the exit.<br/><br/>Third Grave Dead Ahead is the third installment of the Charley Davidson series by Darynda Jones. Charley once again is pulled into a murder case, this time involving a possessive doctor and his missing wife. She’d like to b</span>
  <span id="freeText13127972336371327309" style="display:none"><a href="http://vampirenovelfan.wordpress.com/2012/10/14/third-grave-dead-ahead-charley-davidson-3-dead-on-arrival/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <b>Dead on Arrival…</b>
</a><br /><br />I’m starting to wonder how many more directions we’ll get to these graves. Right, left, ahead… I don’t even know if Charley knows where she’s going anymore. I just hope the cemetery isn’t that big. Personally, I just want to know the directions to the exit.<br /><br />Third Grave Dead Ahead is the third installment of the Charley Davidson series by Darynda Jones. Charley once again is pulled into a murder case, this time involving a possessive doctor and his missing wife. She’d like to be at her best, but after binding Reyes Alexander Farrow (Son of Satan and her lifelong protector) to his body, she’s haunted by him in her sleep, meaning she’s getting no rest at all. So she’ll just solve that little issue by staying awake. I go on record to say that Reyes is a better problem to have than Freddie Kruger…<br /><br />Unable to rely on Reyes’s help when faced with grave danger, she may actually need to take care of herself! Oh the shock!<br /><br />After reading this book, the events of book 2 were rendered completely pointless. Reyes goes from wanting his body to die (since it’s just a burden and he’d only rot in prison) to now wanting to save it to prove his innocence. Deux ex Machina much? He couldn’t have decided on that one <i>whole</i> book prior to this? There’s an excuse, but it’s as thin as the paper these books are printed on. Furthermore, I am completely apathetic to their relationship, and now he’s becoming a lot more of a problem than a sweet escape. Maybe in about 10 books from now they’ll actually fight, or do something way more interesting than what’s here.<br /><br />At this point these books feel really formulaic. There are constant punchlines (very few actually made me laugh), no poignant drama, more humans causing trouble (as if they should be an actual threat to the Grim Reaper), and we get breadcrumbs at best for any development that relates to Charley’s powers. I honestly ended up skimming to the dialogue to get through this book, making me realize that I simply do not like Charley.<br /><br />Finally the last 10% picks up in the paranormal department, but it should have happened a lot sooner. But of course, Charlie has to figure these things out for herself; it cannot be told. She’s just not smart enough to figure it out before the end.<br /><br />I am still scratching my head as to how she didn’t figure out how to reverse a particular spell when the solution ended up being…oh, I don’t know…ONLY THE MOST OBVIOUS THING TO SAY!!<br /><br />I gave three books a go. I really wanted to like it, but at this point this series is not for me. Where’s that exit again? Oh, here it is!<br /><br />*Review also posted to <a href="http://www.amazon.com/review/R271BBEFXR7KTX/ref=cm_cr_rdp_perm" rel="nofollow noopener">Amazon</a>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="13127972336371327309" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        rated it

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2114686239" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16377165556448057557"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“But give up my business? The same business I'd built from the ground up with my own two hands and designer Louis Vuittons? The same business for which I'd sacrificed blood, sweat, and tears? Well, maybe not sweat and tears, but there was blood. Lots of blood. Give it up? Not likely. Besides, what else would I do? I totally should've gone to Hogwarts when I had the chance.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>Here I am, back again on this Charley Davidson bike...See what I did there? Like Harley Davidson?<br/> There's also a</span>
  <span id="freeText16377165556448057557" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“But give up my business? The same business I'd built from the ground up with my own two hands and designer Louis Vuittons? The same business for which I'd sacrificed blood, sweat, and tears? Well, maybe not sweat and tears, but there was blood. Lots of blood. Give it up? Not likely. Besides, what else would I do? I totally should've gone to Hogwarts when I had the chance.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Here I am, back again on this Charley Davidson bike...See what I did there? Like Harley Davidson?<br> There's also a biker-gang in this novel, so this is double-y pun-tastic. Ha, that's a good joke. It is! Ugh, whatever. You'll see!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1504629941ra/23794879.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>*clears throat*<br><br>In the latest (to me) Charley adventure there's a missing person, a shady client, a biker-gang that may be murderous, her dad trying to force her into a new profession, and of course, as always, Reyes Farrow - the super sexy Son of Satan. Oh, and Wong...forever in the corner. <br><br>This book was delightful, really. Each new book, each new hardship forces Charley to become more and more. She's funnier, tougher, wittier. And she's a legit P.I. If you're paying attention, Charley isn't as surface as you could chalk her up to being. She's running this bitch. She's a Bawse. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1504629941ra/23794880.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But I gotta say, on the flip side, I find Reyes to be increasingly rape-y. He's so rape-y, in fact, that Charley is spaced out on coffee and uppers for basically this whole novel, because every time she closes her eyes Reyes shows up and, like, gets super rape-y with her. <br><br>I know everyone is all <i>ohhhhlalala</i> about their relationship, but honestly does no one else see how rape-y he is?! It's makes me so uncomfortable. Charley can't even <i>sleep</i>, people! Seriously, fuck this Son of Satan bitch. He doesn't have much of a personality outside of being a dickhole either. Always growling <i>Charley!</i> like she's a dog he's training. SatanBoy, talk to me like that one time...One time! Anyway, I don't really like him, is what I'm trying to say (Welcome to this week's edition of <i>Unpopular Opinion's with Krystin.)</i> <br><br>And while we're on it, fuck her dad too. All these douchebag men trying to act like they can run her life better than she can. Pshhhhh, bitch please. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Never trust a man with a penis.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Anyway, aside from the consent issue, I loved this because I'm here for Charley - for her sarcastic venom, her view of life and death, her friendships and ghosts; her bumbling her way through each new case with heart and determination, even as all the trouble that seems to find her puts her back in the hospital again. She's got backbone and grit and she knows herself. She takes ownership of her unique abilities, she embraces them with pride and excitment, and she doesn't give a <i>fuckkkkkk</i> whether anyone disapproves of her life. She's gonna live it the way she wants to. And ain't no man gonna stop her! You'll see! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1504629941ra/23794879.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sooooo yeah....this book is definitely fun, a perfect way to spend some precious reading time. It feels like an important installment for Charley's journey. She's really coming into her own. For their genre, these books are my favourite.</span>
  <a data-text-id="16377165556448057557" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<span id="freeTextContainer17032673864547685880">This is actually the first book in the series that I've read, but it was fairly smooth sailing despite that fact. It did take me a while to get used to the quirky/corny humor. But I have to say, I enjoyed the time I spent with Charley, Reyes, Cookie, Garrett and the others. Don't let the silly humor fool you. Darynda Jones writes a good quality mystery story.<br/><br/>Reviewed for Affaire de Coeur in the February 2012 Issue. <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://affairedecoeur.com'>http://affairedecoeur.com</a>.</span>

Darynda Jones writes a good quality mystery story.<br /><br />Reviewed for Affaire de Coeur in the February 2012 Issue. <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://affairedecoeur.com">http://affairedecoeur.com</a>.</span>

<div id="review_220999408" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/220999408" />
    <a title="SubterraneanCatalyst" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5306164-subterraneancatalyst"><img alt="SubterraneanCatalyst" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1306967745p2/5306164.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/220999408?book_show_action=true">Oct 09, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="SubterraneanCatalyst" class="user" itemprop="url" name="SubterraneanCatalyst" href="/user/show/5306164-subterraneancatalyst">SubterraneanCatalyst</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781250008701" href="/book/show/12275623-third-grave-dead-ahead">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5306164-subterraneancatalyst?shelf=cannot-freaking-wait">cannot-freaking-wait</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5306164-subterraneancatalyst?shelf=more-please">more-please</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5306164-subterraneancatalyst?shelf=angels">angels</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5306164-subterraneancatalyst?shelf=paranormal-romance">paranormal-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5306164-subterraneancatalyst?shelf=ghosts">ghosts</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5306164-subterraneancatalyst?shelf=demons">demons</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer220999408" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3971796806840728279">I enjoy reading about Charley and her adventures with Cookie and the hot steaming tease that is Reyes. This book was better than the other two installments because we're getting more information about what Charley really is- we know she's a Grim Reaper. But what else is she capable of? Reyes has been hinting at this since the last book I believe and although that isn't expounded upon in detail here- we do get to see where this whole train is headed toward.<br/><br/><b>Reyes</b>:<img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380360900i/711807._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>[I don't know who this man is..he'</span>
  <span id="freeText3971796806840728279" style="display:none">I enjoy reading about Charley and her adventures with Cookie and the hot steaming tease that is Reyes. This book was better than the other two installments because we're getting more information about what Charley really is- we know she's a Grim Reaper. But what else is she capable of? Reyes has been hinting at this since the last book I believe and although that isn't expounded upon in detail here- we do get to see where this whole train is headed toward.<br><br><b>Reyes</b>:<img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380360900i/711807._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>[I don't know who this man is..he's a model for Dolce &amp; Gabbana though and a close approximation of what I think Reyes might look like]<br>Do you get enough Reyes in this book? I'd say maybe- but he'll also piss you off, I know he pissed me off. I find this acceptable though because you know- he's the Son of Satan and all. He's bound to be at least a little tricky, somewhat dark, and not such a lovey dovey pansy right? Charley doesn't let you down. She's a woman in love but she's not a complete dunce. Amen to that.<br><br><b>Garrett</b>: <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380360900i/711808.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> [This is Wentworth Miller and who I imagine Garrett to be, I think he has enough intensity for Garrett's hard ass ways] I enjoyed Garrett so much more in this book than I ever have. Jones gives you many surprises and fun times with our lovely Garrett. While he's not a love interest, he is flirt worthy, protective and reliably straight laced and the straight man to Charley's quirk and Reyes' insidious beauty and scheming. I think I liked him almost..probably..it's hard for me to confess this, better than Reyes in this book! <br><br><b>The Plot and other Characters</b>:<br>Fun case with sitcom (but better) humor. I guessed a lot of it before I was 2/3rds in the book. Not a big problem except the "clue" seemed to be blinking with a big sign above it "I'M THE MURDER WEAPON! BINGO!". Some readers might also get tired of Charley's flippancy. I didn't..it made me laugh a lot, but it might annoy some readers. <br><br>Mrs. Marigold: Sort of a letdown. Not a huge one but the scene could have been better and further embellished upon.<br><br>Cookie: She really needs to get laid. That is all.<br><br>The Guardian: Sweet, but I have mixed feelings. <br><br>This was a fast read..almost too fast. Of course I'm a fan and I couldn't wait to get through this but I feel like maybe the book should have been longer. Maybe I'm wrong, maybe I'm just too quick of a reader and I devoured this like chocolate laced with crack. <br><br>No cliffhanger but you will definitely feel like you are ready for the next book NOW YESTERDAY WRITE FASTER JONES NOW.<br><br>Bottom Line: If you like Charley and you've liked the other books, you will also like this a whole lot, read it. <br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="3971796806840728279" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2135084362?book_show_action=true">Sep 25, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/12871681-third-grave-dead-ahead">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=challenge-2017-rlftci">challenge-2017-rlftci</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=series-c">series-c</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=genre-romance-paranormal">genre-romance-paranormal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=m-library-sf-e-book">m-library-sf-e-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=authors-d">authors-d</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2459470-lisa-kay?shelf=authors-j">authors-j</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2135084362" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2937609836124490021"><blockquote>
  <i>Quote at the beginning of Chapter 2</i>
  <br/>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1506393145p8/3626101.jpg' height='170' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</blockquote>★★★½✩ While I love Lorelei King, who narrates the audiobook with a wonderful tone of sarcasm, I also got the Kindle version from the library and ending up going with that one for the majority of the book, so I won’t review the audiobook.<br/><br/>Okay, so it has been about five years since I read the last book in this series. Wow; time flys. I had to go back a review the “buddy reads” threads I participated in for the first two books to recall all the character</span>
  <span id="freeText2937609836124490021" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>Quote at the beginning of Chapter 2</i>
  <br>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/photos/1506393145p8/3626101.jpg" height="170" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote>★★★½✩ While I love Lorelei King, who narrates the audiobook with a wonderful tone of sarcasm, I also got the Kindle version from the library and ending up going with that one for the majority of the book, so I won’t review the audiobook.<br><br>Okay, so it has been about five years since I read the last book in this series. Wow; time flys. I had to go back a review the “buddy reads” threads I participated in for the first two books to recall all the characters and plot lines. I will say what I thought then: while these books are very good, it often seems as if Darynda Jones is writing one plot line then switches midstream to another. I wouldn’t say they are plot twists... they actually feel to me like her mind decided to go off in another creative direction. And DJ is creative. I do enjoy her writing style and her humor, though.<br><br>I am a little stumped by Reyes and Charley’s relationship, but then, what else is new? If I was baffled before, I am more so now. I do think Charley matures in this installment, which is refreshing, but she’s suddenly worried about just what Reyes is? Huh? There is some sadness, too, which I felt coming in #2. Just a warning for you. Hopefully, things will look better in #4.<br><br>Love the red tennies on the cover. ☺ </span>
  <a data-text-id="2937609836124490021" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer546053982" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8024591694576604622">This whole book made me sleepy...well, except some of the Reyes scenes!! The problem is Charley is refusing to sleep and things are getting pretty crazy. Every time she goes to sleep, Reyes shows up and he is angry. Granted he wants her but he doesn't want to want her and Charley doesn't like that. Who can blame her? <br/><br/>I'm not sure what it is about this series but it has sucked me in. I love all the snark, I love how dangerous and angry Reyes is, I love how crazy Garrett is and how sweet Cookie is</span>
  <span id="freeText8024591694576604622" style="display:none">This whole book made me sleepy...well, except some of the Reyes scenes!! The problem is Charley is refusing to sleep and things are getting pretty crazy. Every time she goes to sleep, Reyes shows up and he is angry. Granted he wants her but he doesn't want to want her and Charley doesn't like that. Who can blame her? <br /><br />I'm not sure what it is about this series but it has sucked me in. I love all the snark, I love how dangerous and angry Reyes is, I love how crazy Garrett is and how sweet Cookie is. I could just go on and on. <br /><br />Of course, there's drama. There's a new case with a missing person and another case that involves Reyes. Both of them were very intriguing but sometimes all the puzzle pieces get a little confusing. <br /><br />We get to meet the biker gang that owns the asylum and that brought us some new and interesting characters. I'm not sure what to make of Donovan or where that is going to go but I sure do love Artemis and I <i>definitely</i> loved where that went! <br /><br />Mistress Marigold finally makes an appearance and she is as mysterious as ever. It's amazing the things she comes up. <br /><br />The ending was all kinds of crazy! I can't believe all the things that went on. I was so happy that Charley finally took a stand and although I don't like how it came about, I'm really curious to see what impact it will have. My heart went out to Garrett but I liked how that played out...I only wonder what he will remember. I can't wait to read the next book! <br /><br /><br />Favorite quotes:<br /><br />♦ If at first you don’t succeed, skydiving is NOT for you. —BUMPER STICKER<br /><br />♥ "You look good in wet."<br /><br />♥ “My goodness. Garrett on one end and Reyes on the other. It’s like a really hot, melty s’more.”<br /><br />♦ An integral part of any best friend’s job is to immediately clear your computer history if you die. —T-SHIRT<br /></span>

<div id="review_270425736" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/270425736" />
    <a title="Ferdy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy"><img alt="Ferdy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1487898103p2/4596358.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/270425736?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ferdy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ferdy" href="/user/show/4596358-ferdy">Ferdy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9780749956141" href="/book/show/10980787-third-grave-dead-ahead">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=daddy-issues-mummy-issues">daddy-issues-mummy-issues</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=dark-tortured-broody-hero">dark-tortured-broody-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=decent-heroine">decent-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4596358-ferdy?shelf=likeable-hero">likeable-hero</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer270425736" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3877899217928071231"><u> <b>Some Spoilers</b> </u><br/><br/>Charley, Danger and Will Robinson are back and better than ever. Charley is trying her best to stay awake to avoid Reyes who is visiting her in her sleep. Reyes is furiuos that Charley bound his incorperal self to his human body, thus leaving him vunerable. Even though he's angry at Charley he can't help smexing her up when he sees her. There's a lot of tension and resentment between Charley and Reyes, both hurting one other in order to protect the other. Unfortunatley for Charley</span>
  <span id="freeText3877899217928071231" style="display:none"><u> <b>Some Spoilers</b> </u><br /><br />Charley, Danger and Will Robinson are back and better than ever. Charley is trying her best to stay awake to avoid Reyes who is visiting her in her sleep. Reyes is furiuos that Charley bound his incorperal self to his human body, thus leaving him vunerable. Even though he's angry at Charley he can't help smexing her up when he sees her. There's a lot of tension and resentment between Charley and Reyes, both hurting one other in order to protect the other. Unfortunatley for Charley, her love life is only one of her problems - her dad wants her to quit her job, Reyes has escaped from prison, Garrett is still tailing her and Charley must find a missing woman who she believes may have been murdered by her husband.<br /><br /><u>The Good</u>: <br /><br />- Charley is strong, smart and funny..she's dedicated to both her PI and Grim Reaper jobs. She rarely whines or feels sorry for herself.<br />- Reyes..I liked him a LOT before but now I LOVE him. He's smart, powerful and sexy without being a total a**hole..although he does have his moments.<br />-Cookie is an awesome best friend, a lot of authors will write crap female characters in order to make their heroine look better..that doesn't happen here..Cookie is a well rounded character - loyal, brave and witty.<br />-Uncle Bob/Ubie isn't as present in this book as earlier books but he's still got Charley's back.. I'm hoping Ubie and Cookie get together.<br />- I love Garrett almost as much as Reyes..I was suprised by his little twist at the end.<br />-Gemma and Charley taking the first baby steps to rebuiding their relationship.<br />-The side characters - Gemma, Angel, Mr Wong, Rocket, Luthor, Donovon and his gang - had strong personalities and depth instead of the usual UF were most side charcters are one dimensional. <br />-The writing flowed well and was pretty hilarious.<br />-The conclusion of the missing wife wasn't predictable. <br /><br /><u>The Not So Good</u>:<br /><br />-Charley's humour in serious situations did get annoying at times.<br />-The reason why Owen Vaughn hated Charley enough to want to kill her was so lame and then Charley apologising to him..WTF?!!..he should be apologising to her..someone trying to kill you is worse than some stupid misunderstanding in high school. Him trying to kill her was such an overreaction..the whole thing was just stupid and Charley trying to make nice with him after he tried to kill her for no good reason..ugh.<br />-Charley's guardian..I wasn't impressed with who it was at the end.<br />-Reyes constantly threatening Charley..enough already..bloody hell, that's no way to treat the woman you supposedly love!! Reyes shows more affection to Amador, Bianca and their kids than he does Charley..all he seems to show Charley is distrust, lust and anger..he needs to start showing a little bit of affection towards her instead of just hornyness and hatred. <br />-Reyes using Charley and it ending up causing Charley a LOT of pain..seriously?!..first her dad and now Reyes.. two men that claim to love her, they should be protecting her..not doing the bloody opposite and putting her in harm's way..I hope Charley doesn't just forgive Reyes in the next book!<br />-Charley's dad is a douche..I was happy to see that his betrayl in the last book wasn't completely forgotten but I think Charley needs to stop making excuses for him.. he doesn't deserve her love and forgiveness.<br />-Cookie needs some lovin!!! Why does Charley get all the fun?!<br />-Charley's stepmother wasn't really in this book and I was hoping that Charley's dad and sister would finally see what a cow she is and stick up for Charley. <br />-Charley doesn't know how to keep her mouth shut.. <b>seriously</b>..all of hell is trying to find her and she just tells everyone she meets that she's the Grim Reaper and that Reyes is the son of Satan..is Charley <b>retarded</b>??!<br />-Mistress Marigold was a let down..I was hoping for some long buried secrets or some sort of hellish conspiracy..not a boring bloody <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[nun <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />I'm looking forward to the next book now that Reyes circumstances have changed.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="3877899217928071231" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer7409636787712171788"><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12043770.Third_Grave_Dead_Ahead__Charley_Davidson___3_' title='Third Grave Dead Ahead (Charley Davidson, #3) by Darynda Jones' rel='nofollow noopener'>Third Grave Dead Ahead</a> is the third installment in <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4175419.Darynda_Jones' title='Darynda Jones' rel='nofollow noopener'>Darynda Jones</a>'s paranormal mystery series titled: <u>Charley Davidson</u>. Charley is our heroine in this series, and she is in fact the Grim Reaper. I love this concept! ...and I love her! Charley is just an amazing heroine! She's got attitude, loyalty, a wild sense of humor, and a real-life dream man. Yep, sexy, sexy dream man...<br/><br/>The series as a whole presents an ongoing story line that would be best enjoyed in order; however, there is a separate myst</span>
  <span id="freeText7409636787712171788" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/12043770.Third_Grave_Dead_Ahead__Charley_Davidson___3_" title="Third Grave Dead Ahead (Charley Davidson, #3) by Darynda Jones" rel="nofollow noopener">Third Grave Dead Ahead</a> is the third installment in <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/4175419.Darynda_Jones" title="Darynda Jones" rel="nofollow noopener">Darynda Jones</a>'s paranormal mystery series titled: <u>Charley Davidson</u>. Charley is our heroine in this series, and she is in fact the Grim Reaper. I love this concept! ...and I love her! Charley is just an amazing heroine! She's got attitude, loyalty, a wild sense of humor, and a real-life dream man. Yep, sexy, sexy dream man...<br><br>The series as a whole presents an ongoing story line that would be best enjoyed in order; however, there is a separate mystery presented in each book. After all, Charley works a day job as a private investigator as a front for her real line of work. There are tons of characters who make both exits and entrances in each installment so you never get bored with anyone during the series. I loved the first book, the second book was OK, and this third one is back on track and has me already looking for the next installment. If you haven't tried this series yet, you've got to check it out!<br><br><b>My favorite quote:</b><br><i>"I strode towards Mr. Coffee with lust in my eyes. We'd had a thing, Mr. Coffee and I, and there was just enough of him left for one more cup. No need to make a fresh pot, to get him all hot and bothered."</i><br><br>The Charley Davidson series includes the following installments: <br>(as of November 2014)<br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/8788554.First_Grave_on_the_Right__Charley_Davidson___1_" title="First Grave on the Right (Charley Davidson, #1) by Darynda Jones" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_186538937" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/186538937" />
    <a title="Christen (GoldiloxReads)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4652961-christen-goldiloxreads"><img alt="Christen (GoldiloxReads)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1485831597p2/4652961.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/186538937?book_show_action=true">Jul 19, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christen (GoldiloxReads)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christen (GoldiloxReads)" href="/user/show/4652961-christen-goldiloxreads">Christen (GoldiloxReads)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer186538937" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4091886737710234720"><br/><b>This review will not contain spoilers for this book, but do not read it you haven't read books 1 and 2 in this series.</b><br/><br/>Another wonderful installment in Darynda Jones' hilarious and sexy Charley Davidson series!<br/><br/><i>Third Grave Dead Ahead</i> begins almost where it left off - with Reyes back in jail and <i>pisssssed</i> at Charley. Since she bound him to his corporeal body he is stuck in jail and can't visit her incorporeally...except that he can. Every time Charley falls asleep he visits her, which would be HOT </span>
  <span id="freeText4091886737710234720" style="display:none"><br /><b>This review will not contain spoilers for this book, but do not read it you haven't read books 1 and 2 in this series.</b><br /><br />Another wonderful installment in Darynda Jones' hilarious and sexy Charley Davidson series!<br /><br /><i>Third Grave Dead Ahead</i> begins almost where it left off - with Reyes back in jail and <i>pisssssed</i> at Charley. Since she bound him to his corporeal body he is stuck in jail and can't visit her incorporeally...except that he can. Every time Charley falls asleep he visits her, which would be HOT except that his visits include a lot of angry stares and growly words (and some other stuff that's not quite as bad...). So Charley has been drinking coffee nonstop and sleeping minimally, which makes for some very funny moments throughout the book. Charley is as snarky as ever, although I felt like she had more serious moments in this book than the other two, and I didn't mind those at all. There are also more Reyes moments in <i>Third Grave</i>, and I mean <i>real</i> Reyes moments, not just <i>incorporeal</i> Reyes moments. To keep from being spoiler-rific, I won't give any more details about that, but just know that all the Reyes that was missing from <i>Second Grave</i> is made up for in this one. <br /><br />Of course there is actually an official investigation that Charley and Cookie are handling (Oh Cookie, how I've missed you as Charley's 'straight man'!), and as always these plot points are just as interesting as the Charley-Reyes stuff. Charley is looking for a missing woman (isn't she always) and that brings in some of the best side characters in the genre: Angel, Rocket, and Garrett. <br /><br />If you loved the first two books in this series you will be thoroughly pleased with this one. All of the things that make this one of my favorite series are here - Charley's silly one liners and ridiculous train of thought, Reyes' <b>hotness and enough Reyes scenes to whet your whistle, a great main plot, and secondary characters that I love love love. This book also moves along the continuing story of Reyes and Charley, and we learn even more about his childhood.<br /><br />If you are new to Charley's world I highly recommend checking out this series. It is a one of a kind and a can't-put-it-down kind of read!<br /><br />Read more of my reviews at goldiloxandthethreeweres.blogspot.com </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="4091886737710234720" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <a title="Alex ☣ Deranged KittyCat ☣" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat"><img alt="Alex ☣ Deranged KittyCat ☣" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1483783358p2/13555222.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1752383679?book_show_action=true">Sep 16, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Alex ☣ Deranged KittyCat ☣" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Alex ☣ Deranged KittyCat ☣" href="/user/show/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat">Alex ☣ Deranged KittyCat ☣</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/12871681-third-grave-dead-ahead">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat?shelf=kick-ass-ladies">kick-ass-ladies</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat?shelf=paranormal-uf">paranormal-uf</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat?shelf=2016-favorites">2016-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat?shelf=adult">adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat?shelf=mystery-thriller-horror">mystery-thriller-horror</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat?shelf=demons">demons</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat?shelf=funny-that">funny-that</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13555222-alex-deranged-kittycat?shelf=ghosts">ghosts</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1752383679" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12524111475982240961"><b>O.M.G!</b> <br/><br/>Full review to come.<br/><br/>*********************************************<br/><br/><b>Actual review</b><br/><br/>Since reading the third book, I went away for the weekend, during which period I have also read the fourth book. I was very disappointed with that one, so I'll do my very best to remember the awesomeness of this one.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474224127ra/20570146.gif' width='460' height='259' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>Lead me not into temptation. I can find it myself. - T-Shirt</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br/><br/>The most important change for me in this book is <b>Reyes</b>. Yes, he's the Big Bad and the supermodel son of Satan, but I prefer him</span>
  <span id="freeText12524111475982240961" style="display:none"><b>O.M.G!</b> <br><br>Full review to come.<br><br>*********************************************<br><br><b>Actual review</b><br><br>Since reading the third book, I went away for the weekend, during which period I have also read the fourth book. I was very disappointed with that one, so I'll do my very best to remember the awesomeness of this one.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474224127ra/20570146.gif" width="460" height="259" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>
    <blockquote>Lead me not into temptation. I can find it myself. - T-Shirt</blockquote>
  </b>
</i><br><br>The most important change for me in this book is <b>Reyes</b>. Yes, he's the Big Bad and the supermodel son of Satan, but I prefer him in the flesh. His projection can go so far, and the only way his projection and Charley can have any action is if he takes hold of her soul. But a man made of flesh and blood is a whole other thing. A real touch, a real breath on the neck... priceless. And I rooted for him like crazy. That is until near the end, where his plot is uncovered. Why do the men in Charley's life keep doing that to her? And why does she stand it? Ok, it's clear she would eventually forgive them, but at least let her make a scene, a real scene, where she cuts deeply into their feelings if not into their flesh. But I think I'm slipping into the next book here. <b>Stars, the anger!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1450817099ra/17472132.gif" width="500" height="260" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As for <b>Charley</b>, of course she's as cool as ever. I think Darynda Jones should write a manual about how to get Davidson's coolness and her good use of sarcasm. That book would sell, too. There's nothing better than saying the right thing at the right time, and giving little crap about the other person's feelings.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1474225048ra/20570220.gif" width="500" height="208" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And I need to give the author extra credit for not letting me figure out who the guardian is.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1460676789ra/18773530.gif" width="500" height="279" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>That being said, I need to take a one day break before writing the review for the next Charley Davidson book. I had serious issues with that one. &gt;.&lt;</span>
  <a data-text-id="12524111475982240961" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2141654136" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2141654136" />
    <a title="Angela (Angel&#39;s Guilty Pleasures)" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7742509-angela-angel-s-guilty-pleasures"><img alt="Angela (Angel&#39;s Guilty Pleasures)" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1463631966p2/7742509.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2141654136?book_show_action=true">Oct 03, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Angela (Angel&#39;s Guilty Pleasures)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Angela (Angel&#39;s Guilty Pleasures)" href="/user/show/7742509-angela-angel-s-guilty-pleasures">Angela (Angel&#39;s Guilty Pleasures)</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook " href="/book/show/13450678-third-grave-dead-ahead">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7742509-angela-angel-s-guilty-pleasures?shelf=3-stars">3-stars</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2141654136" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17519608530084768298">Many have recommend the <i>Charley Davidson</i> series to me and now I’ve finally picked it up. I’ve been really enjoying this series and how things are progressing. The series does need to be read or listened to in order. <br/><br/><b>Third Grave Dead Ahead</b> is full of mysteries, betrayals, heartache, and revelations. <br/><br/>There is a lot going on in this installment; with three different mystery’s happening, understanding exactly what Charley can do, and Charley now trying to get in and out of the asylum without the bik</span>
  <span id="freeText17519608530084768298" style="display:none">Many have recommend the <i>Charley Davidson</i> series to me and now I’ve finally picked it up. I’ve been really enjoying this series and how things are progressing. The series does need to be read or listened to in order. <br><br><b>Third Grave Dead Ahead</b> is full of mysteries, betrayals, heartache, and revelations. <br><br>There is a lot going on in this installment; with three different mystery’s happening, understanding exactly what Charley can do, and Charley now trying to get in and out of the asylum without the biker club catching her.<br><br>The overall plot moved along well and now I know a bit more about Charley and her abilities, though we are not finished learning what she can do as the Grim Reaper. Their is much more to discover. I love the friendship Charley has with Cookie. Cookie is a great secondary character and just adds to the story. The witty humor continues to be fun, but at times if feel like Charley uses it to mask her stupid mistakes or maybe it’s her way of copping with a difficult and stressful situation. I do have to say I was rolling my eyes at some of the things Charley did in this one and I will point out that I didn’t care for how this one started, dream sex. Other then that I had fun and enjoyed the story and progress happening. <br><br>Reyes of course plays a part in the story. He’s got his own agenda in <i>Third Grave Dead Ahead</i> and once Charley figures it out, it’s almost too late. Then to top it off she’s got her investigations and her family to deal with. She really hasn’t had it easy and dons’t have many people on her side. I was angry and sad for Charley. The men in her life really upset me. What Reyes and her father do, really made me sad. <br><br><b>The Narrator,</b> Lorelei King continues to make this series enjoyable. She does an outstanding job bringing Charley to life and all the characters. I continue to appreciate and like the audio version for this series. <br><br><i>If you enjoy snarky humor and a good mystery then give the Charley Davidson series a try. I highly recommend the audio version for the series.</i> <br><br><b>Rated: 3.5 Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://angelsguiltypleasures.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1466193893i/19451911.jpg" width="400" height="100" alt="angelsgp-seethisreview-blure" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17280901842967881367">UF goodness continues. <br/><br/>No, Charlie isn't Gaiman's Death, nor is she a Reaper from Bleach. She IS, however, an Unknown Quantity who still believes she's Normal Folk. <br/><br/>That, with the snark and the UF goodness of solving murders with supernatural powers, the wicked (often truly so) reveals from people she trusts the most, and the whole general STAY AWAKE AT ALL COSTS vibe... it manages to come down to earth quite nicely.<br/><br/>That, and I don't blame her son-of-Satan boyfriend for being super pissed at her</span>
  <span id="freeText17280901842967881367" style="display:none">UF goodness continues. <br /><br />No, Charlie isn't Gaiman's Death, nor is she a Reaper from Bleach. Or for her being super pissed at him. Different reasons, different times, but damn... AT LEAST THEY STILL HAVE CHEMISTRY. :)<br /><br />I'm having a really good time with this.</span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer2593611635" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3314678606429586873">Poor Charley. This girl gets betrayed by more people. It’s really sad because she is the most loyal person, like ever. Always sticking her neck out for everyone. I can’t wait to read the next book. I honestly don’t know how Reyes and Charley can ever be together after everything that’s happened. They both do too many things to hurt each other. It’s baffling because we also know how much they love each other. </span>

          </span>
        </div>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GBWEjDSduVqCTyGXWglsrP7kxzYG1oNtq+97NcZ6YwPxySGPjPd/v58Y2zQgj9iLUn6mT5RUQrUSkA0R1bbesw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('mukZEBJJYaaKIrLIUKJvlPNlj+x2VmozKxo+zEZNWh5zNbwTqiOnQ5d1SGsqJNuzX//uleTUq+uSZUjoVYHnrg==')})
  }
//]]>

  <span id="freeText9154064044508820943" style="display:none">NYTimes and USA Today Bestselling Author Darynda Jones has won numerous awards for her work, including a prestigious RITA, a Golden Heart, and a Daphne du Maurier, and her books have been translated into 17 languages. As a born storyteller, Darynda grew up spinning tales of dashing damsels and heroes in distress for any unfortunate soul who happened by, certain they went away the better for it. She penned the international bestselling Charley Davidson series and is currently working on several beloved projects, most notably the Sunshine Vicram Mystery Series with St. Martin's Press and the Betwixt and Between Series of paranormal women's fiction. She lives in the Land of Enchantment, also known as New Mexico, with her husband and two beautiful sons, the Mighty, Mighty Jones Boys. <br /><br />Click here to read one of the more popular short stories by Darynda called The Monster:<br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://theneverneath.com/2018/02/02/the-monster-part-1/">https://theneverneath.com/2018/02/02/...</a><br /><br />She can be found at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.daryndajones.com">http://www.daryndajones.com</a></span>
